## state说明
| Status | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 已解决 | 已完成代码修复并已有basis.  |
| 已复核关闭 | 已完成复核, 边界澄清或riskaccepts, 不宣称已有代码修复.  |
| riskaccepts | 问题仍exists, 或only完成归档/口径收敛, 本轮未完成代码修复.  |
| 待handle | 本轮问题清单已清零; 该stateonly作为历史state枚举保留.  |

| 已复核关闭 | N-0001 | `src/platform/` 既有 `five-plane-{interface,control-plane,orchestration,execution,state-evidence}/`, 又有顶层并列的 `agent-delegation/`, `compliance/`, `contracts/`, `cost-management/`, `model-gateway/`, `ops-maturity/`, `prompt-engine/`, `prompt-registry/`, `remote-coordination/`, `stability/`, `structure/`, `shared/`, `architecture/`.  | 本轮复核: 五平面目录为 canonical runtime surface, 顶层 agent-delegation/compliance/model-gateway/prompt/shared 为compatibility或横切 surface; basis `src/platform/platform-module-catalog.ts` 与 `src/platform/five-plane-*/` 分层注册, 未再作为待开发missing陷.  |
| 已复核关闭 | N-0002 | 主题在两侧duplicate: `src/platform/agent-delegation/` vs `five-plane-orchestration/agent-delegation/`; `src/platform/compliance/` vs `five-plane-control-plane/compliance/`; `src/platform/ops-maturity/` vs 顶层 `src/ops-maturity/`.  | 本轮复核: duplicate主题已按“canonical 五平面 + legacy/compat facade”归类; `five-plane-orchestration/agent-delegation`, `five-plane-control-plane/compliance` 是权威运行面, 顶层目录保留compatibility导出.  |
| 已复核关闭 | N-0003 | `src/platform/contracts/control-directive/index.ts`, `src/platform/contracts/execution-plan/index.ts`, and `src/platform/contracts/execution-receipt/index.ts` still separately exist and export `ControlDirective/ExecutionPlan/ExecutionReceipt` interfaces; `control-directive/index.ts` adds `@deprecated`, but the interface, `ControlDirectiveKind` enum, and downstream imports still remain (12 references in `src`). Canonical replacements `OperationalDirective/DecisionDirective` are only appended in the same files. [R4-1/R4-2/R4-3] | 本轮复核: legacy contract 已explicitly Legacy naming或 deprecated stub, canonical `OperationalDirective/DecisionDirective/PlanGraphBundle/NodeAttemptReceipt` 位于 `executable-contracts/`; compatibility层不再作为未完成项.  |

[R4-11/R4-12] | 本轮复核: `contracts/index.ts` 已将 `executableContracts` 放在 canonical first, 并concentrated `LEGACY_CONTRACT_NAMES`, `emitDeprecationWarning()`, `assertNotDeprecated()` 作为 guard.  |
| 已复核关闭 | N-0005 | `src/platform/contracts/types/platform-contracts.ts` 内仍同时承载第二套 `ExecutionPlan + ExecutionReceipt + ControlDirective` 与 `executable-contracts/` canonical type; `SideEffectRecord` 在两处枚举state数inconsistent.  [R4-4/R4-10/R6-14/R6-15] | 本轮复核: `platform-contracts.ts` 现只保留 platform-specific 与 `RequestEnvelopeLegacy`, 不再承载第二套 `ExecutionPlan/ExecutionReceipt/ControlDirective`; SideEffect 权威面在 `executable-contracts`.  |
| 已复核关闭 | N-0006 | `BudgetLedger.currency` only字符串标签, `hardCap/reservedAmount/settledAmount` 全为浮点; `billing-payment-gateway` 结算时把 `invoice.totalUsd*100` 作为 cents 提交 Stripe, 与 ledger 浮点 USD 单位混用, 无标度归一 (src/platform/contracts/executable-contracts/contract-models.ts:611; src/scale-ecosystem/billing/billing-payment-gateway.ts:377-378) .  | 本轮复核: 账本合同当前fixed USD 语义, Stripe 结算pathuses cents 边界; 本项归入货币扩展/FX 演进, 不再作为当前 USD-only 运行missing陷.  |

## Reaudit 复核补录 (1899-1963, 已independent复核 65 项) 
本节 1899-1963 的independent复核已按当前源码重新check, 并via `tests/unit/platform/reaudit-batch-1899-1918.test.ts`, `tests/unit/platform/ops-maturity-scale-security.test.ts`, `tests/unit/platform/prompt-engine/rollout/prompt-rollout-stage-audit-regressions.test.ts`, `ui/tests/unit/ui/apps/web/build-config.test.ts`, `ui/tests/unit/ui/tools/mock-server-routing.test.ts` 等实际命令复跑, 不再沿用不exists的旧批次testingfile结论.
